# IT Service Module - Complete Specification Document

**Project**: ProjectFlows - IT Service Request Management Module
**Version**: 1.0.0
**Date**: 2025-10-31
**Status**: Planning & Design Phase

### üìù Recent Updates (2025-11-01) ‚≠ê **UPDATED**

**Phase 2 Progress - IT Service Portal UI** (2025-11-01 Session 2)
- ‚úÖ **Task 1: IT Service Layout** - Enhanced with USER role isolation
  - USER role redirect system (login ‚Üí IT Service, blocked from dashboard)
  - Clean layout for USER (no sidebar) for profile/settings pages
  - Back button and menu item for returning to IT Service portal
  - ITServiceTopBar with ProjectFlows logo and fiscal year filter

- ‚úÖ **Task 2: Sidebar Navigation** - Badge count with role-based scope filtering
  - "IT Service" menu (all roles)
  - "‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠" menu (management roles only) with pending count badge
  - Role-based request filtering: USER/MEMBER/HEAD ‚Üí department, LEADER ‚Üí division, CHIEF ‚Üí mission group

- ‚úÖ **Task 3: Portal Page** - COMPLETE
  - ‚úÖ 3 action cards with lucide icons (Database, Code, Wrench)
  - ‚úÖ Request cards list in sidebar (desktop) and below cards (mobile)
  - ‚úÖ Filters UI (type, status, search, myRequests toggle)
  - ‚úÖ Responsive design (mobile: 1 col, tablet: 2 cols, desktop: 3 cols + sidebar)
  - ‚úÖ Request forms (COMPLETE - Phase 2 Task 4)
  - ‚ùå Document preview (pending - Phase 2 Task 5)

**UI/UX Enhancements**:
- Centered action cards with increased spacing
- Removed unnecessary text (headers, descriptions)
- Simplified filter controls (removed fiscal year section from sidebar)
- Mobile-responsive layout (action cards stack vertically, request list below)
- Touch-friendly card sizing on mobile devices

**Enhancement 1: Queue System** (Previous)
- FIFO (First In First Out) queue calculation by request type
- Real-time queue position display with progress bar
- Estimated wait time based on historical data
- 3 display locations: Portal cards list, Tracking page, Management table

**Enhancement 2: Satisfaction Rating System** (Previous)
- 1-10 star rating system for completed requests
- Optional comment field for suggestions (max 1000 chars)
- Analytics dashboard with rating distribution, trends, and export

## Database Schema Design

### Schema Changes Overview

‡∏à‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° **7 tables** ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà + ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç **1 enum** ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö

**Tables**:
1. UserRole enum - ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç (‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° SUPER_ADMIN)
2. ServiceRequest - ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ (‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å)
3. RequestTimeline - ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏î‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
4. RequestComment - ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô
5. RequestApprover - ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
6. SystemSettings - ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö
7. **ServiceRequestFeedback** ‚≠ê **NEW** - ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏û‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à

### 1. Enum: UserRole (‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç)

```prisma
enum UserRole {
  SUPER_ADMIN  // ‚≠ê NEW - Highest privilege
  ADMIN
  CHIEF
  LEADER
  HEAD
  MEMBER
  USER
}
```

**‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏ú‡∏•**: SUPER_ADMIN ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô role ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö + ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î/‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î modules

---

### 2. Table: ServiceRequest (‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å)

```prisma
model ServiceRequest {
  id                String              @id @default(cuid())
  requestNumber     String              @unique // ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ö‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô (auto-generate: SR-2025-00001)
  type              ServiceRequestType  // DATA, PROGRAM, IT_ISSUE
  fiscalYear        Int                 // ‡∏õ‡∏µ‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì (2568, 2569, etc.) - CRITICAL for filtering

  // ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á (‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å users table)
  requesterId       String
  requesterName     String              // Snapshot: titlePrefix + firstName + lastName
  requesterJobTitle String?             // Snapshot: jobTitle
  requesterDivision String?             // Snapshot: division name
  requesterPhone    String?             // Snapshot: internalPhone
  requesterEmail    String              // Snapshot: email

  // ‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏∑‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á
  subject           String              // ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á
  description       String              // ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î
  purpose           String?             // ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏ñ‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πå (DATA/PROGRAM only)
  purposeOther      String?             // ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏ñ‡∏∏‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πå‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô‡πÜ (DATA/PROGRAM only)
  deadline          Int?                // ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô (DATA/PROGRAM only)
  issueTime         DateTime?           // ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤ (IT_ISSUE only)

  // ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
  approverId        String?
  approverName      String?             // Snapshot when approved
  approverJobTitle  String?             // Snapshot when approved
  approvedAt        DateTime?

  // ‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞
  status            RequestStatus       @default(PENDING)

  // ‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£
  documentHtml      String              @db.Text // HTML content ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö print

  // Task ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏á
  taskId            String?             @unique

  // Timestamps
  createdAt         DateTime            @default(now())
  updatedAt         DateTime            @updatedAt

  // Relations
  requester         User                @relation("RequestRequester", fields: [requesterId], references: [id])
  approver          User?               @relation("RequestApprover", fields: [approverId], references: [id])
  task              Task?               @relation("RequestTask", fields: [taskId], references: [id])
  timeline          RequestTimeline[]
  comments          RequestComment[]
  feedback          ServiceRequestFeedback?  // ‚≠ê NEW: One-to-one feedback

  @@index([requesterId])
  @@index([approverId])
  @@index([status])
  @@index([type])
  @@index([createdAt])
  @@map("service_requests")
}

enum ServiceRequestType {
  DATA        // ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
  PROGRAM     // ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏°
  IT_ISSUE    // ‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤ IT
}

enum RequestStatus {
  PENDING         // ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
  APPROVED        // ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
  REJECTED        // ‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ò
  IN_PROGRESS     // ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏î‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£
  COMPLETED       // ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡∏™‡∏¥‡πâ‡∏ô
  CANCELLED       // ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏Å
}
```

**Design Decisions**:
- ‚úÖ **Snapshot Pattern**: ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• requester/approver ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô snapshot ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á
- ‚úÖ **Conditional Fields**: ‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏•‡∏î‡πå‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó (nullable)
- ‚úÖ **Document HTML**: ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö HTML ‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö print (regenerate ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠)
- ‚úÖ **Unique taskId**: 1 request = 1 task maximum

---

### 3. Table: RequestTimeline (‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥)

```prisma
model RequestTimeline {
  id           String              @id @default(cuid())
  requestId    String
  type         RequestTimelineType

  // ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏î‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ (optional - ‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ actor)
  actorId      String?
  actorName    String?             // Snapshot: fullName
  actorJobTitle String?            // Snapshot: jobTitle
  actorAvatar  String?             // Snapshot: profileImageUrl

  // ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î
  description  String              // ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏≠‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå
  metadata     Json?               // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏° (oldStatus, newStatus, etc.)

  createdAt    DateTime            @default(now())

  // Relations
  request      ServiceRequest      @relation(fields: [requestId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  actor        User?               @relation("TimelineActor", fields: [actorId], references: [id])

  @@index([requestId])
  @@index([createdAt])
  @@map("request_timeline")
}

enum RequestTimelineType {
  CREATED           // ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á
  VIEWED            // ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏≠‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô
  APPROVED          // ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
  REJECTED          // ‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ò
  TASK_CREATED      // ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á task ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß
  TASK_ASSIGNED     // ‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô
  TASK_UPDATED      // ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏û‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô
  COMMENTED         // ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô
  COMPLETED         // ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡∏™‡∏¥‡πâ‡∏ô
  CANCELLED         // ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏Å
}
```

**Design Decisions**:
- ‚úÖ **Event Sourcing Pattern**: ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å event ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏Ç‡∏∂‡πâ‡∏ô
- ‚úÖ **Actor Snapshot**: ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏î‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô snapshot
- ‚úÖ **Flexible Metadata**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ JSON ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ event type

### 4. Table: RequestComment (‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô)

```prisma
model RequestComment {
  id          String         @id @default(cuid())
  requestId   String
  userId      String
  content     String         @db.Text
  createdAt   DateTime       @default(now())
  updatedAt   DateTime       @updatedAt

  // Relations
  request     ServiceRequest @relation(fields: [requestId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)
  user        User           @relation("RequestComments", fields: [userId], references: [id])

  @@index([requestId])
  @@index([userId])
  @@index([createdAt])
  @@map("request_comments")
}
```

**Design Decisions**:
- ‚úÖ **Simple Structure**: ‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏¢ task comments
- ‚úÖ **Cascade Delete**: ‡∏•‡∏ö request ‚Üí ‡∏•‡∏ö comments ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î

---

### 5. Table: RequestApprover (‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥)

```prisma
model RequestApprover {
  id              String              @id @default(cuid())
  userId          String
  approvalType    ApprovalType        // DATA, PROGRAM, IT_ISSUE
  isActive        Boolean             @default(true)
  createdAt       DateTime            @default(now())
  updatedAt       DateTime            @updatedAt

  // Relations
  user            User                @relation("UserRequestApprovers", fields: [userId], references: [id])

  @@unique([userId, approvalType])  // 1 user ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏°‡∏µ 1 approval type ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß
  @@index([userId])
  @@index([approvalType])
  @@index([isActive])
  @@map("request_approvers")
}

enum ApprovalType {
  DATA        // ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•
  PROGRAM     // ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏°
  IT_ISSUE    // ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤ IT
}
```

**Design Decisions**:
- ‚úÖ **Granular Permissions**: ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥ 3 ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó
- ‚úÖ **Unique Constraint**: 1 user ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥ approval type
- ‚úÖ **Soft Disable**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ isActive ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô delete

---

### 6. Table: SystemSettings (‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö)

```prisma
model SystemSettings {
  id            String    @id @default(cuid())
  key           String    @unique
  value         String    @db.Text
  description   String?
  updatedBy     String?
  updatedAt     DateTime  @updatedAt

  // Relations
  updater       User?     @relation("SystemSettingsUpdater", fields: [updatedBy], references: [id])

  @@index([key])
  @@map("system_settings")
}

// Default settings to seed:
// - "IT_SERVICE_ENABLED": "true" | "false"
// - "HOSPITAL_NAME": "‡πÇ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏û‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏•‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏¢‡∏†‡∏π‡∏°‡∏¥" (example)
```

**Design Decisions**:
- ‚úÖ **Key-Value Store**: ‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏î‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏∏‡πà‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° settings ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢
- ‚úÖ **Audit Trail**: ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î

---

### 7. Table: ServiceRequestFeedback (‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏û‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à) ‚≠ê **NEW**

```prisma
model ServiceRequestFeedback {
  id                String         @id @default(cuid())
  serviceRequestId  String         @unique  // One feedback per request
  rating            Int            // ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏û‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à 1-10 ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏ß
  comment           String?        @db.Text // ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏° (optional)
  createdAt         DateTime       @default(now())
  updatedAt         DateTime       @updatedAt

  // Relations
  serviceRequest    ServiceRequest @relation(fields: [serviceRequestId], references: [id], onDelete: Cascade)

  @@index([serviceRequestId])
  @@index([rating])
  @@index([createdAt])
  @@map("service_request_feedback")
}
```

**Design Decisions**:
- ‚úÖ **One feedback per request**: ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `@unique` constraint ‡∏ö‡∏ô serviceRequestId
- ‚úÖ **Editable**: Requester ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (updatedAt ‡∏à‡∏∞ track)
- ‚úÖ **Rating 1-10**: ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢ (10 ‡∏Ñ‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏°)
- ‚úÖ **Optional comment**: ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö
- ‚úÖ **Analytics-ready**: ‡∏°‡∏µ indexes ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö query rating trends

**Validation Rules**:
```typescript
interface FeedbackValidation {
  rating: number;       // Required, min: 1, max: 10
  comment?: string;     // Optional, max: 1000 characters
}
```

**Business Rules**:
1. ‚úÖ Requester ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ feedback ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ `status = COMPLETED`
2. ‚úÖ Requester ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç feedback ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ï‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤
3. ‚úÖ ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ SUPER_ADMIN/ADMIN ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô feedback ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á request ‡∏≠‡∏∑‡πà‡∏ô
4. ‚úÖ Feedback rating ‚â§ 3 ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏ß ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏™‡πà‡∏á notification ‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á SUPER_ADMIN/ADMIN
5. ‚úÖ ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ feedback ‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (enforce by @unique constraint)

**Notification Trigger**:
```typescript
// ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ rating ‚â§ 3 ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏ß (low satisfaction)
if (feedback.rating <= 3) {
  notifySuperAdmins(
    "SERVICE_REQUEST_LOW_RATING",
    `‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á ${requestNumber} ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô ${rating} ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏ß - ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö`,
    `/it-service/feedback?requestId=${requestId}`
  );
}
```

---

### Relations Summary

**User Relations** (‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô users table):
```prisma
model User {
  // ... existing fields

  // ‚≠ê NEW: IT Service Relations
  serviceRequests       ServiceRequest[]    @relation("RequestRequester")
  approvedRequests      ServiceRequest[]    @relation("RequestApprover")
  requestApprovers      RequestApprover[]   @relation("UserRequestApprovers")
  requestComments       RequestComment[]    @relation("RequestComments")
  requestTimeline       RequestTimeline[]   @relation("TimelineActor")
  systemSettingsUpdates SystemSettings[]    @relation("SystemSettingsUpdater")
}
```

**Task Relations** (‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ô tasks table):
```prisma
model Task {
  // ... existing fields

  // ‚≠ê NEW: Service Request link
  serviceRequest  ServiceRequest?  @relation("RequestTask")
}
```

---

### Database Indexes Strategy

**High Priority Indexes** (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏ö‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢):
- ‚úÖ `service_requests.requesterId` - filter by user
- ‚úÖ `service_requests.status` - filter by status
- ‚úÖ `service_requests.type` - filter by type
- ‚úÖ `service_requests.createdAt` - sort by date
- ‚úÖ `request_timeline.requestId` - fetch timeline
- ‚úÖ `request_approvers.userId + approvalType` - check permissions

**Composite Indexes** (‡∏û‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ performance ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏î‡∏µ):
- `service_requests(status, createdAt)` - pending requests sorted by date
- `service_requests(requesterId, status)` - user's requests by status

---

## API Endpoints Specification

### Base Path
```
/api/service-requests
```

### Authentication
‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å endpoint ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `withAuth()` middleware ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Bearer token

---

### Endpoint List (16 endpoints)

#### 1. System Settings

**GET /api/system-settings**
- **Purpose**: ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö
- **Auth**: SUPER_ADMIN only
- **Response**:
```typescript
{
  success: true,
  data: {
    IT_SERVICE_ENABLED: boolean,
    HOSPITAL_NAME: string
  }
}
```

**PATCH /api/system-settings**
- **Purpose**: ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö
- **Auth**: SUPER_ADMIN only
- **Body**:
```typescript
{
  IT_SERVICE_ENABLED?: boolean,
  HOSPITAL_NAME?: string
}
```

- **Auth**: SUPER_ADMIN only
- **Response**:
```typescript
{
  success: true,
  data: {
    approvers: Array<{
      id: string,
      user: {
        id: string,
        fullName: string,
        jobTitle: string,
        email: string
      },
      approvalType: "DATA" | "PROGRAM" | "IT_ISSUE",
      isActive: boolean
    }>
  }
}
```

**POST /api/service-requests/approvers**
- **Purpose**: ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥

```typescript
  userId: string,
```

- **Purpose**: ‡∏•‡∏ö‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
- **Auth**: SUPER_ADMIN only

#### 3. Request Submission (USER)

**POST /api/service-requests**
- **Purpose**: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà
- **Auth**: Authenticated users
- **Body**:
```typescript
{
  type: "DATA" | "PROGRAM" | "IT_ISSUE",
  subject: string,
  description: string,
  purpose?: string,           // DATA/PROGRAM only
  purposeOther?: string,      // DATA/PROGRAM only
  deadline?: number,          // DATA/PROGRAM only
  issueTime?: string,         // IT_ISSUE only (ISO datetime)
}
```
- **Response**:
```typescript
{
  success: true,
  data: {
    request: {
      id: string,
      requestNumber: string,
      type: string,
      status: string,
      documentHtml: string,
      createdAt: string
    }
  }
}
```
- **Logic**:
  1. Validate input ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Zod
  2. Auto-generate requestNumber (SR-YYYY-NNNNN)
  3. Snapshot requester data ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å users table
  4. Generate document HTML ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏°‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö
  5. Create request
  6. Create timeline entry (CREATED)
  7. Send notification ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á approvers

---

#### 4. Request Listing

**GET /api/service-requests**
- **Purpose**: ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á
- **Auth**:
  - USER: ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á
  - Approvers: ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô requests ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° approval type
  - ADMIN/SUPER_ADMIN: ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î
- **Query Params**:
```typescript
{
  type?: "DATA" | "PROGRAM" | "IT_ISSUE",
  status?: "PENDING" | "APPROVED" | ...,
  startDate?: string,  // ISO date
  endDate?: string,    // ISO date
  page?: number,       // default: 1
  limit?: number       // default: 20
}
```
- **Response**:
```typescript
{
  success: true,
  data: {
    requests: Array<{
      id: string,
      requestNumber: string,
      type: string,
      subject: string,
      status: string,
      requesterName: string,
      createdAt: string
    }>,
    pagination: {
      total: number,
      page: number,
      limit: number,
      totalPages: number
    }
  }
}
```

**GET /api/service-requests/:id**
- **Purpose**: ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á
- **Auth**:
  - Requester ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á request ‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô
  - Approver ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå
  - ADMIN/SUPER_ADMIN
- **Response**:
```typescript
{
  success: true,
  data: {
    request: {
      id: string,
      requestNumber: string,
      type: string,
      subject: string,
      description: string,
      purpose?: string,
      deadline?: number,
      issueTime?: string,
      status: string,
      documentHtml: string,
      requesterName: string,
      requesterJobTitle: string,
      requesterDivision: string,
      requesterPhone: string,
      requesterEmail: string,
      approverName?: string,
      approverJobTitle?: string,
      approvedAt?: string,
      taskId?: string,
      createdAt: string,
      updatedAt: string
    }
  }
}
```
- **Logic**:
  1. Check permission
  2. Fetch request with relations
  3. Create timeline entry (VIEWED) if approver opens

#### 5. Request Approval (Approvers)

**POST /api/service-requests/:id/approve**
- **Purpose**: ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á
- **Auth**: Approvers with matching approval type
- **Response**:
```typescript
{
  success: true,
  data: {
    request: { ... },
    task: {
      id: string,
      name: string,
      projectId: string
    }
  }
}
```
- **Logic**:
  1. Check approver permission
  2. Update request status = APPROVED
  3. Snapshot approver data
  4. Create Task automatically:
     - Name: ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á[type] #[requestNumber] - [subject]
     - Description: Link to request + ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î
     - Priority: 2 (High)
     - StatusId: Default project status
  5. Link task to request
  6. Create timeline entries (APPROVED, TASK_CREATED)
  7. Send notification to requester

**POST /api/service-requests/:id/reject**
- **Purpose**: ‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ò‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á
- **Auth**: Approvers with matching approval type
- **Body**:
```typescript
{
  reason: string
}
```
- **Logic**:
  1. Check approver permission
  2. Update request status = REJECTED
  3. Create timeline entry (REJECTED) with reason
  4. Send notification to requester

```typescript
{
  success: true,
```

- **Auth**: Requester, Task assignees, Approver
- **Body**:
```typescript
{
  content: string
}
```
- **Logic**:
  1. Create comment
  2. Create timeline entry (COMMENTED)
  3. Send notification ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡∏µ

**GET /api/service-requests/:id/comments**
- **Purpose**: ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á comments ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á

#### 7. Queue System

**GET /api/service-requests/:id/queue**
- **Purpose**: ‡∏î‡∏π‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á (USER ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á)
- **Auth**:
  - Requester ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á request ‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô
  - Approver ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå
  - ADMIN/SUPER_ADMIN
- **Response**:
```typescript
{
  success: true,
  data: {
    queuePosition: number,     // ‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô 3)
    totalInQueue: number,      // ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô 8)
    approverName: string,      // ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
    estimatedWaitTime: string, // ‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô "1-2 ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô")
    status: string             // ‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô
  }
}
```
- **Logic**:
  1. Filter requests ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° type (DATA, PROGRAM, IT_ISSUE)
  2. Filter ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ status = PENDING
  3. Sort ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° createdAt ASC (FIFO - First In First Out)
  4. ‡∏´‡∏≤ position ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á request ‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô queue
  5. ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì estimatedWaitTime ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢ historical data
  6. ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ lastKnownQueuePosition ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô ‚Üí create timeline entry (QUEUE_UPDATED)

---

#### 8. Task Integration

**PATCH /api/tasks/:taskId**
- **Extension**: ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ task ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ serviceRequest link ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å update
- **Logic ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏°**:
  1. ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ update status ‚Üí create timeline entry (TASK_UPDATED)
  2. ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ close task ‚Üí update request status = COMPLETED
  3. ‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ assign user ‚Üí create timeline entry (TASK_ASSIGNED)

---

#### 9. Feedback System (‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏û‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à) ‚≠ê **NEW**

**POST /api/service-requests/:id/feedback**
- **Purpose**: ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏û‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à
- **Auth**: Requester only
- **Validation**:
  - Request must have `status = COMPLETED`
  - Only requester can submit feedback
  - Rating: 1-10 (required)
  - Comment: max 1000 characters (optional)
- **Request Body**:
  ```typescript
  {
    rating: number;     // 1-10 stars
    comment?: string;   // Optional feedback text
  }
  ```
- **Response**:
  ```typescript
  {
    success: true,
    data: {
      feedback: {
        id: string,
        serviceRequestId: string,
        rating: number,
        comment: string | null,
        createdAt: string,
        updatedAt: string
      }
    }
  }
  ```
- **Business Logic**:
  1. Upsert feedback (create if not exists, update if exists)
  2. If rating ‚â§ 3: notify SUPER_ADMIN/ADMIN
  3. Create timeline entry: "FEEDBACK_SUBMITTED"
  4. Return feedback data

**GET /api/service-requests/:id/feedback**
- **Purpose**: ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• feedback ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á request
- **Auth**: Requester, Approver, ADMIN, SUPER_ADMIN
- **Response**:
  ```typescript
  {
    success: true,
    data: {
      feedback: ServiceRequestFeedback | null
    }
  }
  ```
- **Business Logic**:
  - Return null if no feedback yet
  - Check permission: only requester, approvers, or admins

**GET /api/service-requests/feedback/stats**
- **Purpose**: ‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏¥ feedback ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö SUPER_ADMIN Dashboard
- **Auth**: SUPER_ADMIN, ADMIN only
- **Query Params**:
  ```typescript
  {
    type?: "DATA" | "PROGRAM" | "IT_ISSUE";  // Filter by request type
    startDate?: string;   // ISO date
    endDate?: string;     // ISO date
    departmentId?: string;  // Filter by department
  }
  ```
- **Response**:
  ```typescript
  {
    success: true,
    data: {
      stats: {
        totalFeedbacks: number,
        averageRating: number,  // Overall average (0-10)
        ratingDistribution: {
          1: number,  // Count of 1-star ratings
          2: number,
          // ... up to 10
        },
        byType: {
          DATA: { count: number, avgRating: number },
          PROGRAM: { count: number, avgRating: number },
          IT_ISSUE: { count: number, avgRating: number }
        },
        trend: [
          { month: string, avgRating: number, count: number }
        ],
        lowRatings: [  // Feedbacks with rating ‚â§ 3
          {
            requestId: string,
            requestNumber: string,
            rating: number,
            comment: string,
            createdAt: string
          }
        ]
      }
    }
  }
  ```
- **Business Logic**:
  1. Apply filters (type, date range, department)
  2. Calculate average rating
  3. Group by rating (1-10)
  4. Calculate trend (monthly aggregation)
  5. Find low-rated requests (rating ‚â§ 3)

**GET /api/service-requests/feedback/export**
- **Purpose**: Export feedback data as CSV
- **Auth**: SUPER_ADMIN, ADMIN only
- **Query Params**: Same as stats endpoint
- **Response**: CSV file download
- **CSV Columns**:
  - Request Number
  - Request Type
  - Requester Name
  - Department
  - Rating (1-10)
  - Comment
  - Feedback Date
  - Completion Date

---

### API Response Standards

‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å endpoint ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ `successResponse()` ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ `errorResponse()` helper:

```typescript
// Success
{
  success: true,
  data: { ... },
  message?: string
}

// Error
{
  success: false,
  error: {
    code: "ERROR_CODE",
    message: "Human-readable message"
  }
}
```

### Error Codes

| Code | HTTP | Description |
|------|------|-------------|
| `UNAUTHORIZED` | 401 | ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏•‡πá‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏ô |
| `FORBIDDEN` | 403 | ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á |
| `NOT_FOUND` | 404 | ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏û‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• |
| `INVALID_INPUT` | 400 | ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• input ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á |
| `MODULE_DISABLED` | 403 | IT Service module ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô |
| `APPROVER_REQUIRED` | 403 | ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô approver ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô |

---

## UI/UX Design

### Design Principles

‚úÖ **Consistency** - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ design system ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏≠‡∏û‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å (shadcn/ui)
‚úÖ **Simplicity** - USER ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏°
‚úÖ **Responsiveness** - ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö desktop (>= 768px) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ mobile (< 768px)
‚úÖ **Thai-first** - ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° terminology ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î
‚úÖ **Accessibility** - WCAG 2.1 Level AA compliant

---

### Navigation Strategy

#### Sidebar Menu Integration

**‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° Menu Item ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà**: "IT Service" (‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏§‡∏©‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á‡πÜ ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠)

```typescript
// src/components/layout/sidebar.tsx - mainNavigation array
const mainNavigation = [
  {
    name: "‡πÅ‡∏î‡∏ä‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏£‡πå‡∏î",
    href: "/dashboard",
    icon: LayoutDashboard,
    enabled: true,
    requiredRoles: [],
  },
  {
    name: "‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô",
    href: "/department/tasks",
    icon: CheckSquare,
    enabled: true,
    requiredRoles: [],
  },
  {
    name: "‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πå",
    href: "/projects",
    icon: FolderKanban,
    enabled: true,
    requiredRoles: ["ADMIN", "CHIEF", "LEADER", "HEAD"],
  },
  // ‚≠ê NEW - IT Service Menu
  {
    name: "IT Service",
    href: "/it-service",
    icon: Headphones, // or HelpCircle, Server, Zap (lucide-react)
    enabled: true,
    requiredRoles: [], // All roles can access
  },
  {
    name: "‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠",
    href: "/it-service/manage",
    icon: FileText,
    enabled: true,
    requiredRoles: ["ADMIN", "CHIEF", "LEADER", "HEAD"], // Approvers only
    badge: "dynamic", // Show pending count
  },
  {
    name: "‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô",
    href: "/reports",
    icon: BarChart3,
    enabled: true,
    requiredRoles: ["ADMIN", "CHIEF", "LEADER", "HEAD", "MEMBER"],
  },
  {
    name: "‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏£",
    href: "/users",
    icon: Users,
    enabled: true,
    requiredRoles: ["ADMIN", "CHIEF", "LEADER", "HEAD"],
  },
];
```

**Menu Behavior by Role**:

| Role | Sees "IT Service"? | Sees "‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠"? | Destination |
|------|-------------------|------------------|-------------|
| **USER** | ‚úÖ Yes | ‚ùå No | `/it-service` (Portal) |
| **MEMBER** | ‚úÖ Yes | ‚ùå No | `/it-service` (Portal) |
| **HEAD+** | ‚úÖ Yes | ‚úÖ Yes (with badge) | `/it-service` (Portal) |
| **Approver** | ‚úÖ Yes | ‚úÖ Yes (with badge) | `/it-service` (Portal) |
| **ADMIN/SUPER_ADMIN** | ‚úÖ Yes | ‚úÖ Yes (with badge) | `/it-service` (Portal) |

**Badge Logic for "‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠"**:
```typescript
// Fetch pending count
const { data } = useRequestsPendingCount();
// Show badge: (3) or (12+) if > 99

<Badge variant="destructive">{count > 99 ? '99+' : count}</Badge>
```

**When Used**:
- MEMBER/HEAD/LEADER/ADMIN/SUPER_ADMIN clicks "IT Service" menu
- Uses regular dashboard layout with sidebar
- Keeps navigation accessible

**Implementation**:
```typescript
// src/app/(dashboard)/it-service/layout.tsx (NEW)
export default function ITServiceLayout({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) {
  const { user } = useAuth();

  // USER role gets clean layout
  if (user?.role === 'USER') {
    return <ITServiceCleanLayout>{children}</ITServiceCleanLayout>;
  }

  // Other roles get regular dashboard layout
  return <>{children}</>;
}
```

**Key Differences**:
- ‚ùå **USER**: No Sidebar - Clean minimalist interface
- ‚úÖ **Non-USER**: Regular Sidebar - Full navigation available
- ‚úÖ **Custom Top Bar** (USER only) - Logo "IT Service" ‡πÅ‡∏ó‡∏ô "ProjectFlows"
- ‚úÖ **Auto-redirect** (USER only) - Login ‚Üí IT Service Portal

### Page Designs

### Queue System Design

#### Overview

‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á USER ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥ ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ USER ‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏£ ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤

#### Queue Calculation Logic

**‡∏™‡∏π‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì**:
```typescript
Queue Position = COUNT(requests WHERE:
  - status = PENDING
  - type = same_type (DATA/PROGRAM/IT_ISSUE)
  - createdAt < current_request.createdAt
) + 1

Example:
- Request A (DATA): createdAt 10:00 ‚Üí Queue: 1
- Request B (DATA): createdAt 10:05 ‚Üí Queue: 2
- Request C (PROGRAM): createdAt 10:10 ‚Üí Queue: 1 (different type)
- Request D (DATA): createdAt 10:15 ‚Üí Queue: 3
```

**Key Points**:
- ‚úÖ ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° request type (DATA, PROGRAM, IT_ISSUE)
- ‚úÖ ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á (FIFO - First In First Out)
- ‚úÖ ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ PENDING status ‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô
- ‚úÖ Update real-time ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏µ request ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥

#### API Endpoint

**GET /api/service-requests/:id/queue**
- **Purpose**: ‡∏î‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß
- **Auth**: Requester, Approver, ADMIN
- **Response**:
```typescript
{
  success: true,
  data: {
    queuePosition: number,        // ‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß (1, 2, 3, ...)
    totalInQueue: number,         // ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î (same type)
    estimatedWaitTime: string?,   // (Optional) ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠ "1-2 ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô"
    approverName: string?,        // ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥
    status: "PENDING" | "APPROVED" | ...
  }
}

// Example Response:
{
  success: true,
  data: {
    queuePosition: 3,
    totalInQueue: 8,
    estimatedWaitTime: "1-2 ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô",
    approverName: "‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏¢ ‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏ç‡∏°‡∏µ ‡∏î‡∏µ",
    status: "PENDING"
  }
}
```

```typescript
        ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏õ‡πà‡∏ß‡∏¢

          ‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà {queuePosition} / {totalInQueue}

        <Badge variant="success">‚úÖ ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß</Badge>
```

**Component Structure**:
```typescript
// src/components/it-service/queue-status-card.tsx
interface QueueStatusProps {
  queuePosition: number;
  totalInQueue: number;
  approverName?: string;
  estimatedWaitTime?: string;
  status: RequestStatus;
}

export function QueueStatusCard({
  queuePosition,
  totalInQueue,
  approverName,
  estimatedWaitTime,
  status
}: QueueStatusProps) {
  if (status !== 'PENDING') return null;

  const progress = ((queuePosition - 1) / totalInQueue) * 100;

  return (
    <Card className="border-yellow-200 bg-yellow-50 dark:bg-yellow-950/20">
      <CardHeader>
        <CardTitle className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Clock className="h-5 w-5 text-yellow-600" />
          ‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß
        </CardTitle>
      </CardHeader>
      <CardContent className="space-y-4">
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
          <div>
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì</p>
            <p className="text-3xl font-bold text-yellow-600">
              {queuePosition} / {totalInQueue}
            </p>
          </div>
          {approverName && (
            <div>
              <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å</p>
              <p className="text-sm font-medium">{approverName}</p>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {estimatedWaitTime && (
          <div>
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠</p>
            <p className="text-sm font-medium">{estimatedWaitTime}</p>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Progress Bar */}
        <div>
          <div className="flex justify-between text-xs mb-1">
            <span>‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤</span>
            <span>{Math.round(progress)}%</span>
          </div>
          <Progress value={progress} className="h-2" />
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1">
            ‡∏°‡∏µ {queuePosition - 1} ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì
          </p>
        </div>
      </CardContent>
    </Card>
  );
}
```

---

**Location 3: Timeline Entry (Auto-update)**

‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô ‚Üí ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á timeline entry ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥:

```
31/10/25 10:15 : üìù ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏Ç SR-2025-00123 ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö
                 ‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏à‡∏à‡∏∏‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô: 5 / 12
    ‚Üì
31/10/25 10:30 : ‚¨ÜÔ∏è ‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô: 4 / 11
                 (‡∏°‡∏µ 1 ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥)
    ‚Üì
31/10/25 10:45 : ‚¨ÜÔ∏è ‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô: 3 / 10
    ‚Üì
31/10/25 11:00 : ‚¨ÜÔ∏è ‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô: 2 / 9
```

**Timeline Entry Type**:
```typescript
// Add to RequestTimelineType enum
enum RequestTimelineType {
  CREATED,
  VIEWED,
  APPROVED,
  REJECTED,
  TASK_CREATED,
  TASK_ASSIGNED,
  TASK_UPDATED,
  COMMENTED,
  COMPLETED,
  CANCELLED,
  QUEUE_UPDATED,  // ‚≠ê NEW - Queue position changed
}
```

**Auto-create Logic**:
```typescript
// When any PENDING request of same type is approved/rejected
async function updateQueuePositions(approvalType: 'DATA' | 'PROGRAM' | 'IT_ISSUE') {
  // Get all pending requests of this type
  const pendingRequests = await prisma.serviceRequest.findMany({
    where: {
      type: approvalType,
      status: 'PENDING'
    },
    orderBy: { createdAt: 'asc' }
  });

  // Create timeline entry for each if position changed
  for (const [index, request] of pendingRequests.entries()) {
    const newPosition = index + 1;
    const oldPosition = request.lastKnownQueuePosition; // Store in DB

    if (oldPosition && oldPosition !== newPosition) {
      // Position changed - create timeline entry
      await prisma.requestTimeline.create({
        data: {
          requestId: request.id,
          type: 'QUEUE_UPDATED',
          description: `‡∏•‡∏≥‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô: ${newPosition} / ${pendingRequests.length}`,
          metadata: {
            oldPosition,
            newPosition,
            totalInQueue: pendingRequests.length
          }
        }
      });

      // Update last known position
      await prisma.serviceRequest.update({
        where: { id: request.id },
        data: { lastKnownQueuePosition: newPosition }
      });
    }
  }
}
```

#### Database Schema Addition

‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏ü‡∏¥‡∏•‡∏î‡πå‡πÉ‡∏ô `ServiceRequest` table:

```prisma
model ServiceRequest {
  // ... existing fields

  // ‚≠ê NEW - Queue tracking
  lastKnownQueuePosition Int?  // ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ detect changes

  // ... relations
}
```

#### Estimated Wait Time Calculation (Optional - Advanced)

```typescript
// Calculate based on historical data
async function calculateEstimatedWaitTime(
  requestType: 'DATA' | 'PROGRAM' | 'IT_ISSUE',
  queuePosition: number
): Promise<string | null> {
  // Get average approval time for last 30 days
  const thirtyDaysAgo = new Date();
  thirtyDaysAgo.setDate(thirtyDaysAgo.getDate() - 30);

  const approvedRequests = await prisma.serviceRequest.findMany({
    where: {
      type: requestType,
      status: 'APPROVED',
      approvedAt: { gte: thirtyDaysAgo }
    },
    select: {
      createdAt: true,
      approvedAt: true
    }
  });

  if (approvedRequests.length === 0) return null;

  // Calculate average time from creation to approval (in hours)
  const totalHours = approvedRequests.reduce((sum, req) => {
    const diffMs = req.approvedAt!.getTime() - req.createdAt.getTime();
    return sum + diffMs / (1000 * 60 * 60);
  }, 0);

  const avgHoursPerRequest = totalHours / approvedRequests.length;

  // Estimate wait time = avgHours * queuePosition
  const estimatedHours = avgHoursPerRequest * queuePosition;

  // Convert to human-readable
  if (estimatedHours < 4) return "‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ";
  if (estimatedHours < 24) return "‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô 1 ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô";
  if (estimatedHours < 48) return "1-2 ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£";
  if (estimatedHours < 120) return "2-5 ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£";
  return "‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ 5 ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£";
}
```

#### Queue System Benefits

‚úÖ **Transparency** - USER ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πà‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á
‚úÖ **Expectation Management** - ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
‚úÖ **Fairness** - FIFO principle ‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ò‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°
‚úÖ **Real-time Updates** - Timeline ‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏¥‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô
‚úÖ **Motivation** - ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å progress bar

#### 2. Request Form Modal

**Trigger**: ‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏Å "‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•/‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏°" ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ "‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤ IT"

**Design Pattern**: Modal (shadcn Dialog) ‡∏Ç‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏î Large

**Form Layout - ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•/‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏°**:

**Document Styling** (CSS):
```css
@media print {
  /* Show only document content when printing */
  body * { visibility: hidden; }
  .document-print-area, .document-print-area * {
    visibility: visible;
  }
  .document-print-area {
    position: absolute;
    left: 0;
    top: 0;
    width: 100%;
    font-family: 'Sarabun', sans-serif;
    font-size: 16pt;
    line-height: 1.6;
    page-break-inside: avoid;
  }
}
```

**Font**: Sarabun 16pt (‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á import Google Fonts ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ self-host)

**Timeline Item Component**:
```typescript
<TimelineItem>
  <Avatar src={actorAvatar} />
  <div>
    <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
      <span className="font-semibold">{actorName}</span>
      {actorJobTitle && <span className="text-muted-foreground">({actorJobTitle})</span>}
    </div>
    <div className="text-sm">{description}</div>
    <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{formatDateTime(createdAt)}</div>
  </div>
</TimelineItem>
```

**Status Badges**:
- PENDING: üü° Yellow
- APPROVED: üü¢ Green
- REJECTED: üî¥ Red
- IN_PROGRESS: üîµ Blue
- COMPLETED: ‚úÖ Green with checkmark
- CANCELLED: ‚ö´ Gray

**Responsive (Mobile)**:
- Document preview ‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ (accordion)
- Timeline ‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡πá‡∏°‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≠

### Color Scheme

‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ theme ‡∏™‡∏µ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö ProjectFlows:

| Element | Color | Usage |
|---------|-------|-------|
| Primary | Blue-600 | Buttons, Links, Active states |
| Success | Green-600 | Approved, Completed |
| Warning | Yellow-600 | Pending |
| Danger | Red-600 | Rejected, Cancelled |
| Info | Blue-500 | In Progress |
| Muted | Gray-500 | Secondary text |

**Status Colors**:
```typescript
const statusColors = {
  PENDING: 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800 border-yellow-200',
  APPROVED: 'bg-green-100 text-green-800 border-green-200',
  REJECTED: 'bg-red-100 text-red-800 border-red-200',
  IN_PROGRESS: 'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800 border-blue-200',
  COMPLETED: 'bg-green-100 text-green-800 border-green-200',
  CANCELLED: 'bg-gray-100 text-gray-800 border-gray-200'
};
```

#### 2. Action Card Component

```typescript
// src/components/it-service/action-card.tsx
interface ActionCardProps {
  icon: React.ReactNode;
  title: string;
  description: string;
  color: 'blue' | 'green' | 'purple';
  onClick: () => void;
}

export function ActionCard({ icon, title, description, color, onClick }: ActionCardProps) {
  return (
    <button
      onClick={onClick}
      className={cn(
        "group relative overflow-hidden rounded-lg border p-8",
        "hover:shadow-lg transition-all duration-300",
        "bg-gradient-to-br from-white to-gray-50",
        "dark:from-gray-900 dark:to-gray-800"
      )}
    >
      <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-4 text-center">
        <div className={cn(
          "text-6xl transition-transform group-hover:scale-110",
          colorClasses[color]
        )}>
          {icon}
        </div>
        <h3 className="text-2xl font-semibold">{title}</h3>
        <p className="text-muted-foreground">{description}</p>
      </div>
    </button>
  );
}
```

#### 3. Request Timeline Component

```typescript
// src/components/it-service/request-timeline.tsx
interface TimelineEntry {
  id: string;
  type: string;
  description: string;
  actorName?: string;
  actorJobTitle?: string;
  actorAvatar?: string;
  metadata?: any;
  createdAt: string;
}

export function RequestTimeline({ requestId }: { requestId: string }) {
  const { data, isLoading } = useRequestTimeline(requestId);

  return (
    <div className="space-y-4">
      {data?.timeline.map((entry, index) => (
        <TimelineItem
          key={entry.id}
          entry={entry}
          isLast={index === data.timeline.length - 1}
        />
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}
```

#### 4. Document Template Component

```typescript
// src/components/it-service/document-template.tsx
interface DocumentData {
  requestNumber: string;
  type: 'DATA' | 'PROGRAM' | 'IT_ISSUE';
  // ... other fields
}

export function generateDocumentHtml(data: DocumentData): string {
  const template = data.type === 'IT_ISSUE'
    ? generateITIssueTemplate(data)
    : generateDataProgramTemplate(data);

  return `
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html lang="th">
    <head>
      <meta charset="UTF-8">
      <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Sarabun:wght@400;700&display=swap">
      <style>
        body {
          font-family: 'Sarabun', sans-serif;
          font-size: 16pt;
          line-height: 1.6;
          margin: 2cm;
          text-align: justify;
        }
        .text-center { text-align: center; }
        .indent { text-indent: 2.5cm; }
        /* ... more styles ... */
      </style>
    </head>
    <body>
      ${template}
    </body>
    </html>
  `;
}
```

## Permission System

### New Permissions

‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÑ‡∏õ‡πÉ‡∏ô `src/lib/permissions.ts`:

```typescript
const ROLE_PERMISSIONS = {
  SUPER_ADMIN: ['*'], // ‚≠ê NEW - All permissions

  ADMIN: [
    // ... existing permissions
    'manage_service_requests',    // ‚≠ê NEW - View all requests
  ],

  // ... other roles remain same

  USER: [
    'view_projects',
    'view_tasks',
    'create_service_request',     // ‚≠ê NEW
    'view_own_requests',          // ‚≠ê NEW
    'comment_own_requests',       // ‚≠ê NEW
  ]
};

// ‚≠ê NEW: Check if user is approver
export async function isRequestApprover(
  userId: string,
  requestType: 'DATA' | 'PROGRAM' | 'IT_ISSUE'
): Promise<boolean> {
  const approver = await prisma.requestApprover.findUnique({
    where: {
      userId_approvalType: {
        userId,
        approvalType: requestType
      }
    }
  });

  return approver?.isActive ?? false;
}
```

### Permission Checks

| Action | Who Can Do | Check Method |
|--------|-----------|--------------|
| Enable/Disable Module | SUPER_ADMIN | `role === 'SUPER_ADMIN'` |
| Manage Approvers | SUPER_ADMIN | `role === 'SUPER_ADMIN'` |
| Submit Request | Anyone logged in | `authenticated` |
| View Own Requests | Request owner | `request.requesterId === userId` |
| View All Requests | ADMIN, SUPER_ADMIN | `checkPermission('manage_service_requests')` |
| Approve Request | Assigned approvers | `isRequestApprover(userId, requestType)` |
| View Request | Owner, Approver, ADMIN | Combined check |
| Comment Request | Owner, Task assignees, Approver | Combined check |

### Template Helpers

```typescript
// src/lib/document-helpers.ts

export function formatDateThai(date: Date): {
  day: string;
  month: string;
  year: string;
  buddhistYear: string;
} {
  const thaiMonths = [
    '‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏°', '‡∏Å‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ò‡πå', '‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏°', '‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏©‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ô', '‡∏û‡∏§‡∏©‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏°', '‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ñ‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ô',
    '‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏é‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏°', '‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏°', '‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ô', '‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏°', '‡∏û‡∏§‡∏®‡∏à‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ô', '‡∏ò‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏Ñ‡∏°'
  ];

  return {
    day: date.getDate().toString(),
    month: thaiMonths[date.getMonth()],
    year: date.getFullYear().toString(),
    buddhistYear: (date.getFullYear() + 543).toString()
  };
}

export function generateRequestNumber(): string {
  const now = new Date();
  const year = now.getFullYear();
  const sequence = generateSequenceNumber(); // Auto-increment logic

  return `SR-${year}-${sequence.toString().padStart(5, '0')}`;
}
```

## Implementation Phases

### Phase 1: Database & Backend Foundation (3-4 days)

**Goal**: ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á database schema ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ basic API endpoints

**Tasks**:
1. ‚úÖ Update Prisma schema
   - Add SUPER_ADMIN to UserRole enum
   - Create 5 new tables
   - Add relations to User and Task
   - Generate migration

2. ‚úÖ Create seed data
   - System settings (IT_SERVICE_ENABLED, HOSPITAL_NAME)
   - Sample approvers (at least 3 users)

3. ‚úÖ Implement API endpoints
   - System settings (GET, PATCH)
   - Approvers management (GET, POST, DELETE)
   - Request submission (POST)
   - Request listing (GET with filters)
   - Request detail (GET)

4. ‚úÖ Add permissions
   - Update `src/lib/permissions.ts`
   - Add `isRequestApprover()` helper

**Deliverables**:
- ‚úÖ Prisma schema updated
- ‚úÖ 5 API endpoints working
- ‚úÖ Permission system integrated

## Testing Strategy

### Unit Tests

**Backend**:
- ‚úÖ Request number generation (unique, sequential)
- ‚úÖ Document template generation (correct Thai formatting)
- ‚úÖ Permission checks (approver, owner, admin)
- ‚úÖ Timeline entry creation

**Frontend**:
- ‚úÖ Form validation (required fields, formats)
- ‚úÖ Document preview rendering
- ‚úÖ Timeline rendering
- ‚úÖ Status badge display

### Integration Tests

**API Endpoints**:
```bash
# Request submission flow
POST /api/service-requests ‚Üí 201 Created
GET /api/service-requests ‚Üí 200 OK (list)
GET /api/service-requests/:id ‚Üí 200 OK (detail)

# Approval flow
POST /api/service-requests/:id/approve ‚Üí 200 OK
# Verify: task created, timeline updated, status = APPROVED

# Permission checks
POST /api/service-requests/:id/approve (non-approver) ‚Üí 403 Forbidden
GET /api/service-requests/:id (non-owner) ‚Üí 403 Forbidden
```

### E2E Tests (Manual)

**USER Flow**:
1. ‚úÖ Login as USER ‚Üí redirected to IT Service Portal
2. ‚úÖ Click "‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•/‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏°" ‚Üí form opens
3. ‚úÖ Fill form ‚Üí preview document ‚Üí submit
4. ‚úÖ See request in "My Requests" cards
5. ‚úÖ Click card ‚Üí tracking page opens
6. ‚úÖ Add comment ‚Üí appears in timeline
7. ‚úÖ Print document ‚Üí formatted correctly

**Approver Flow**:
1. ‚úÖ Login as Approver ‚Üí see "‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏≠" in sidebar
2. ‚úÖ Open management page ‚Üí see pending requests
3. ‚úÖ Click request ‚Üí detail modal opens
4. ‚úÖ Approve ‚Üí task created, Task Panel opens
5. ‚úÖ Assign task ‚Üí timeline updated
6. ‚úÖ Verify requester sees update in timeline

**SUPER_ADMIN Flow**:
1. ‚úÖ Login as SUPER_ADMIN ‚Üí access settings
2. ‚úÖ Toggle IT Service module ‚Üí verify USER redirect
3. ‚úÖ Add approver ‚Üí verify user can approve
4. ‚úÖ Change hospital name ‚Üí verify in documents

### Performance Tests

**Targets**:
- ‚úÖ Portal page load: < 1.5s
- ‚úÖ Request submission: < 2s
- ‚úÖ Document preview: < 0.5s
- ‚úÖ Timeline load (50 entries): < 1s
- ‚úÖ API response time: < 200ms (95th percentile)

**Load Tests**:
- 100 concurrent users submitting requests
- 1000 requests in database with pagination
- 500 timeline entries with infinite scroll

## Security Considerations

### Authentication & Authorization

‚úÖ **Session-based auth** - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö authentication ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà
‚úÖ **Permission checks** - ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å API endpoint ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á check permissions
‚úÖ **Row-level security** - USER ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ requests ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏á
‚úÖ **Role-based access** - SUPER_ADMIN, Approvers, USER ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô

### Input Validation

‚úÖ **Zod schemas** - Validate ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å input ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å forms
‚úÖ **SQL injection prevention** - ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Prisma (parameterized queries)
‚úÖ **XSS prevention** - Sanitize HTML output ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô render
‚úÖ **File upload** - (future) Validate file types, size limits

### Data Privacy

‚úÖ **User data snapshot** - ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• requester/approver ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô snapshot
‚úÖ **Audit trail** - Timeline ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å action ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° actor
‚úÖ **Soft deletes** - ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà hard delete requests (‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö audit trail)

## Appendix

### A. Thai Terminology

| English | Thai | Notes |
|---------|------|-------|
| IT Service | ‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏® | ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ module |
| Data/Program | ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•/‡πÇ‡∏õ‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏° | ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó request |
| IT Issue | ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤ IT | ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó request |
| Request Number | ‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏Ç‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÉ‡∏ö‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô | SR-YYYY-NNNNN |
| Tracking | ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô | ‡∏´‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞ |
| Timeline | ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏î‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ | Timeline events |
| Approver | ‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥ | Role ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥ |
| Hospital | ‡πÇ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏û‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏• | Configurable setting |

### B. Database Naming Conventions

- **Table names**: snake_case (e.g., `service_requests`)
- **Column names**: camelCase (e.g., `requesterId`)
- **Enum names**: PascalCase (e.g., `ServiceRequestType`)
- **Enum values**: UPPER_SNAKE_CASE (e.g., `IT_ISSUE`)

### C. API Naming Conventions

- **Endpoints**: kebab-case (e.g., `/api/service-requests`)
- **Query params**: camelCase (e.g., `?startDate=...`)
- **Response fields**: camelCase (e.g., `requestNumber`)

### D. Component Naming Conventions

- **Components**: PascalCase (e.g., `RequestCard`)
- **Files**: kebab-case (e.g., `request-card.tsx`)
- **Folders**: kebab-case (e.g., `it-service/`)
